2, 0, 1, located in that center of all Philadelphia and indeed 
3, 0, 0, at that time 
4, 0, 0, of practically all national finance Third Street and its owners conducted a brokerage business as a side line

6, 0, 0, great and small

8, 0, 0, issuing notes practically without regulation upon insecure and unknown assets and failing and suspending with astonishing rapidity

1, 0, 0, About a year later 
2, 0, 1, Mr Semple died 
3, 0, 0, It was an untimely death 
4, 0, 0, one of those fortuitous and in a way insignificant episodes which are 
5, 0, 0, nevertheless 
6, 0, 0, dramatic in a dull way to those most concerned 
7, 0, 0, He was seized with a cold in the chest late in the fall one of those seizures ordinarily attributed to wet feet or to going out on a damp day 
8, 0, 0, Semple urged him to stay at home and recuperate 
9, 0, 0, He was in his way a very determined person 
10, 0, 0, not obstreperously so 
11, 0, 0, but quietly and under the surface 
12, 0, 0, Business was a great urge 
13, 0, 0, He saw himself soon to be worth about fifty thousand dollars 
14, 0, 0, Then this cold nine more days of pneumonia and he was dead 
15, 0, 0, The shoe store was closed for a few days 
16, 0, 0, the house was full of sympathetic friends and church people 
17, 0, 0, There was a funeral 
18, 0, 0, with burial service in the Callowhill Presbyterian Church 
19, 0, 0, to which they belonged 
20, 0, 0, and then he was buried 
21, 1, 0, Mrs Semple cried bitterly 
22, 0, 0, The shock of death affected her greatly and left her for a time in a depressed state 
23, 0, 0, A brother of hers 
24, 0, 0, David Wiggin 
25, 0, 0, undertook for the time being to run the shoe business for her 
26, 0, 0, There was no will 
27, 0, 0, but in the final adjustment 
28, 0, 0, which included the sale of the shoe business 
29, 0, 0, there being no desire on anybody 's part to contest her right to all the property 
30, 0, 0, she received over eighteen thousand dollars 
31, 0, 0, She continued to reside in the Front Street house 
32, 0, 0, and was considered a charming and interesting widow .
